# Excalidraw Data

## Text Elements
you rewrite in x, find the derivative, write it as reciprocal, replace the y ^hzGbcH55

The change can be measured by hand with the square tecnique with
the derivative, this means that the signed are of the derivative
is the change, when you compare the the function, it does not matter
if you have an extra constant because that is the same in both cases
and therefore taken out, basically even if you translate the two curves
up or down as long as it is by the same ammount there is no impact
on their difference ^OnCvDPku

if you imagine at squares, w is the base and, f of
growing values of n is the height, you sum the area
of the rectangles so b * h, and the thinner the 
rectangles the higher the precision ^9jgW4dS1
